			r1.z = r3.w;
			break;

							r4.xy = float2(1.000000e+000, 1.000000e+000) / r4.xy;
							r4.xy = saturate(r7.xy * r4.xy);
							r7.xy = r4.xy * float2(-2.000000e+000, -2.000000e+000) + float2(3.000000e+000, 3.000000e+000);
							r4.xy = r4.xy * r4.xy;
							r7.zw = r7.xy * r4.xy;
							r6.xyzw = r6.xyzw * g_Global_LightRadiusUVScale[r1.w].xyxy + r3.xyxy;
							r2.z = tShadowMap.SampleCmpLevelZero(PCF_Sampler_s, r6.xy, r3.z).x;
							r1.z = r2.z * r7.z + r1.z;
							r2.z = tShadowMap.SampleCmpLevelZero(PCF_Sampler_s, r6.zw, r3.z).x;
							r2.x = r2.z * r7.w + r2.x;
							r1.xy = r7.xy * r4.xy + r1.xy;
							r5.xyzw = float4(-4.398020e-001, 3.624070e-001, 5.063330e-001, 8.768880e-001) * r5.xyzw;
							r6.xyzw = float4(-1.217193e+000, -8.112668e-001, -6.313437e+000, 1.802704e-002) * g_Global_MinWeightExponent;
							r6.xyzw = exp2(r6.xyzw);
							r4.xy = r6.yw + -r6.xz;
							r6.xy = r0.ww * g_Global_MaxWeight + -r6.xz;
							r4.xy = float2(1.000000e+000, 1.000000e+000) / r4.xy;
							r4.xy = saturate(r6.xy * r4.xy);
							r6.xy = r4.xy * float2(-2.000000e+000, -2.000000e+000) + float2(3.000000e+000, 3.000000e+000);
							r4.xy = r4.xy * r4.xy;
							r6.zw = r6.xy * r4.xy;
							r5.xyzw = r5.xyzw * g_Global_LightRadiusUVScale[r1.w].xyxy + r3.xyxy;
							r0.w = tShadowMap.SampleCmpLevelZero(PCF_Sampler_s, r5.xy, r3.z).x;
							r0.w = r0.w * r6.z + r1.z;
							x22[0].x = r0.w;
							r1.xy = r6.xy * r4.xy + r1.xy;
							x23[0].x = r1.x;
							r0.w = tShadowMap.SampleCmpLevelZero(PCF_Sampler_s, r5.zw, r3.z).x;
							r0.w = r0.w * r6.w + r2.x;
							x22[1].x = r0.w;
							x23[1].x = r1.y;
						}
						r0.w = x22[0].x;
						r1.x = x22[1].x;
						r0.w = r1.x + r0.w;
						r1.x = x23[0].x;
						r1.y = x23[1].x;
						r1.x = r1.x + r1.y;
						r2.y = r0.w / r1.x;
					}
				}
			}
			r0.w = r2.y + -r4.z;
			r0.w = r2.w * r0.w + r4.z;
			r1.x = g_Global_FalloffParams.w == 1.000000;
			r2.xyzw = g_Global_InvView._m10_m11_m12_m13 * r0.zzzz;
			r2.xyzw = r0.yyyy * g_Global_InvView._m00_m01_m02_m03 + r2.xyzw;
			r2.xyzw = r0.xxxx * g_Global_InvView._m20_m21_m22_m23 + r2.xyzw;
			r2.xyzw = g_Global_InvView._m30_m31_m32_m33 + r2.xyzw;
			r0.xyz = r2.xyz / r2.www;
			r0.xyz = g_Global_LightPositionAndRadius.xyz + -r0.xyz;
			r0.xyz = g_Global_LightPositionAndRadius.www * r0.xyz;
			r0.x = dot(r0.xyz, r0.xyz);
			r0.x = sqrt(r0.x);
			r0.x = r0.x * g_Global_FalloffParams.x + g_Global_FalloffParams.y;
			r0.x = max(r0.x, 0.000000000e+000);
			r0.x = -r0.x * r0.x + 1.000000000e+000;
			r0.x = max(r0.x, 0.000000000e+000);
			r0.x = log2(r0.x);
			r0.x = g_Global_FalloffParams.z * r0.x;
			r0.x = exp2(r0.x);
			r0.y = -1.000000000e+000 + r0.w;
			r0.x = r0.x * r0.y + 1.000000000e+000;
			r0.x = r1.x ? r0.x : r0.w;
			r0.y = 1.000000000e+000 + -r0.x;
			r0.x = g_Global_ShadowIntensity * r0.y + r0.x;
			r0.y = r0.x == 1.000000;
			if (r0.y != 0) discard;
			o0.x = r0.x;
		}
	}
	return;
}
